Predoctoral Fellowship Contract Data Science/ Artificial Intelligence	La Salle. Universitat Ramon Llull	Barcelona y alrededores (Presencial)	              La Salle Digital Engineering School, Ramon Llull University (Barcelona) offers a predoctoral fellowship as part of the State Plan for Scientific and Technological Research and Innovation of the Ministry for Science and Technology of the Spanish Government to undertake a PhD thesis in the framework of the funded project:New Physics Searches and Data Challenges with the LHCb experiment at CERN.Summary of the project:LHCb is a particle physics experiment running at CERN‚Äôs Large Hadron Collider (LHC). The LHCb collaboration brings together 1600 members from 96 institutes in 21 different countries.The experiment has been collecting collisions data since 2010. The detector has been upgraded and has started a new phase of data taking in 2022. The experiment was designed to search for physics beyond the Standard Model (SM) of particle physics through precision measurements of CP violation and rare decays of heavy-flavored (beauty and charmed) hadrons produced at the LHC. With the upgraded apparatus, the experiment opens the window to a new and exciting era with a higher discovery potential.Particle physics experiments involve scientific, technological and computational challenges. The change of running conditions in this new data-taking period has implied shifts of paradigm in data-acquisition methods, computing and analysis techniques, which are all challenges in the context of large-scale, global, collaborative and competitive research.The LHCb group of La Salle is involved in applying machine-learning techniques for reconstruction and particle identification, analysis of radiative b-decays, and commissioning and operation of the detector with main focus on the calorimeter detector.Tasks:The PhD thesis work will include the development of new reconstruction and particle identification algorithms for future upgrades of the LHCb detector and detector related tasks. Some short research stays at CERN are also foreseen.The successful candidate will enrol to the doctoral program in Information Technologies and their Application to Management, Architecture and Geophysics of the Ramon Llull University.Research FieldApplied physics, Computer scienceEducation LevelMaster Degree or equivalentSkills/QualificationsMaster degree in the field of Physics, Data Science, AI or similar.To fulfill one of the following criteria to be admitted in a doctoral programme: A Spanish official Bachelor's degree or equivalent, as well as an official university Master's degree or equivalent, provided that a minimum of 300 ECTS credits have been completed with the combination of these degrees.Holder of degrees obtained under foreign education systems within the European Higher Education Area (EHEA), without the need for their homologation, provided that the degree certifies a level 7 on the European Qualifications Framework and grants access to doctoral studies in the country where it was issued.Holder of degrees obtained under non-EHEA foreign education systems, without the need for their homologation, subject to verification by the university that the degree attests to a level of training equivalent to that of the official Spanish university master's degree and grants access to doctoral studies in the country where the degree was issued. Database Engineer (MSA)	Proton | Privacy by Default	Barcelona, Catalu√±a, Espa√±a	              A better internet, where privacy is the default, is possible. Building this better internet might seem daunting or even unthinkable, but at Proton, this is what we do every day.Proton was founded in 2014 by a group of scientists who met at the European Organization for Nuclear Research (CERN). Our first product, Proton Mail, is now the world‚Äôs largest encrypted email service. Subsequent Proton products, such as Proton VPN, Proton Calendar, Proton Drive and Proton Pass give our users full control over how and with whom their data is shared.Today, Proton makes privacy universally accessible. Journalists from outlets like The Guardian and The New York Times , some of the world‚Äôs largest organizations, and people in more than 180 countries have signed up for over 100 million accounts. Our diverse and dynamic team is made up of more than 400 members representing over 40 different nationalities. We need you, your voice, your ideas, and your ambition to make it happen.Purpose of the roleMSA is a highly multi-disciplinary group started in 2019 to tackle difficult mail delivery, spam, abuse, and account security problems that impact the Proton ecosystem. We built sophisticated systems from scratch that combine human intelligence and machine learning to make tens of millions of realtime or asynchronous decisions each day. As of late 2023, our areas of focus are 1) mail delivery and spam, 2) abuse and account security, 3) site reliability of Proton, and 4) a new product involving blockchains. Over the past few years, our custom systems have reduced spam filter misclassifications by over 60%, blocked millions of abusive bulk signups, protected hundreds of thousands of users from account compromise by attackers, and mitigated hundreds of DDoS attacks. In order to move fast with limited resources, we are organized into autonomous teams responsible for the whole system, with expertise across infrastructure, data storage, backend, web and mobile apps, machine learning, security and operational excellence. In 3 years, we grew from 2 engineers to over 30 engineers and analysts, spread across 3 continents for 24/7 coverage. We are looking for humble, mission-driven, systems-thinking people who want to make a big impact in a startup environment.What You Will DoMSA is responsible for the operational excellence of many critical services that must run reliably 24/7 and scale with increasing traffic and complexity. These services depend on various data stores and caches, including MySQL, MongoDB, Postgres, ClickHouse, Ceph and Redis. You will be responsible for: automation, operations, and stress tests involving these database servers, which run in Proton's data centers.make sure the systems have dependable backups, redundant architecture, safe migrations, accurate alerting, and on-call support.  debugging and figuring out problems that inevitably come up in production. Our services are open source, audited, and supported by community contributions. We give back to our community by maintaining core encryption libraries and by supporting other organizations furthering the same goals as us. The team employs diverse methods, such as content classification, workflow automation, entity extraction, and recommender systems, to enhance customer productivity and support our customers, who lead innovation in the world.We are a global team reporting to the director of data science in US. The team culture is about openness, collaboration, excellence, and innovative thinking rooted in domain expertise, fostering creativity and entrepreneurship.
